\hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a584debe9e4020eaffb9dd784c705c74a}{C\+F\+L\+A\+GS}=\char`\"{}-\/g\char`\"{} Using \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a900bb06a4314d99c8ad08d1ceffd114e}{from} My\+S\+QL -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ On \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a10824cd39765967d500aad8915878804}{systems} \hyperlink{group__apr__network__io_ga40101ce9c63cc7ab2b80f6f8c0e7086c}{where} both \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} and My\+S\+QL \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{README_8txt_abf5a4a7b9414b8b9683ee861c8a64879}{installed}, \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a23198464f7594670aa87529673e8496f}{possible} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{README_8txt_a83fd323c6a07ea419cc41fd2d0f1675b}{make} use \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a900bb06a4314d99c8ad08d1ceffd114e}{from} within My\+S\+QL, \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7681723cb91eaa99771ee87f8465c1aa}{as} an alternative \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} the \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a441b0f5d179bd730727fd325dfe75401}{built}-\/\hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a14415789461ee2ace28e34eea786cc6c}{pattern} matching. There \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} web page that tells you \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga6e0837f31f9838d1bc93f4e98184579f}{how} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a29df1716374a8e3439d34a27760970bd}{do} this\+: http\+: Making new tarballs -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ The \hyperlink{README_8txt_ad096865ab7f15682efeeeb3ef7983ae3}{command} \char`\"{}make \hyperlink{README_8txt_aaa00612a17576703fa649e7c2a7da281}{dist}\char`\"{} creates three \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} tarballs, \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} tar.\+gz, \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a08cce63b2b0b9195f79f9b41b954a5e8}{tar.\+bz2}, and zip formats. The \hyperlink{README_8txt_ad096865ab7f15682efeeeb3ef7983ae3}{command} \char`\"{}make distcheck\char`\"{} does the same, but then does \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} trial build \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the new distribution \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} ensure that \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it} works. If you have modified \hyperlink{README_8txt_a117db88886e3b44e72c9457ba51928bc}{any} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a0ccf45b17b45fe5e9f9dbe203ebd801a}{man} page sources \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} the \hyperlink{group__MOD__DAV_gab79aad8aa27988a0e86b9397d43541e8}{doc} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ac33d049ccd70185ffba7bed3d06d9ea2}{directory}, you should \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ae5e6e8bc4bfa800414992418716f96df}{first} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} the Prepare\+Release \hyperlink{basic-configuration_8txt_ac1048f198f179d52eda77c5ed6ab9ba9}{script} before making \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} distribution. This \hyperlink{basic-configuration_8txt_ac1048f198f179d52eda77c5ed6ab9ba9}{script} creates the .\hyperlink{testmemcache_8c_a92b58db5ab4f0133c78fadf9a2fbf439}{txt} and H\+T\+ML forms \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a5c227f81d9a06a8bc0cfd7b51643c528}{documentation} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a900bb06a4314d99c8ad08d1ceffd114e}{from} the \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a0ccf45b17b45fe5e9f9dbe203ebd801a}{man} pages. Testing \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ To test the basic \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7d2e848fb4392b4e74cbf478dbdc6ad1}{library} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_gade8f959a935ed315f9f55422c7de9903}{on} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} Unix-\/like \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_acd344400255173b94380e8f8cdfa5ddc}{system}, \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} the Run\+Test script. There \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a7fa37393a0d2c379953288d92a0dd395}{another} \hyperlink{basic-configuration_8txt_ac1048f198f179d52eda77c5ed6ab9ba9}{script} called Run\+Grep\+Test that \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} the \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aefb1fa742c21909e746b978f6e1d7e17}{options} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the pcregrep command. If the \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ac5c2ebe543528426f0c731e1b7056868}{C}++ wrapper \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7d2e848fb4392b4e74cbf478dbdc6ad1}{library} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a441b0f5d179bd730727fd325dfe75401}{built}, three test programs called pcrecpp\+\_\+unittest, pcre\+\_\+scanner\+\_\+unittest, and pcre\+\_\+stringpiece\+\_\+unittest \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} also built. When J\+IT \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ad138d584026b091836ba441440a66ff5}{support} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{group__APR__Util__Bucket__Brigades_ga03e6cca0c879c0443efb431c30c14f76}{enabled}, \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a7fa37393a0d2c379953288d92a0dd395}{another} test \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a48917cf15a1089461e55bc56de9a58c3}{program} called pcre\+\_\+jit\+\_\+test \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} built. Both the \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab38bb7c8bef8456778ba3b5559de3d0d}{scripts} and \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a0c81554ea08028a00dbedabe60072c53}{all} the \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a48917cf15a1089461e55bc56de9a58c3}{program} \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} \hyperlink{util__expr__scan_8c_aa1a71763978093648dffef60b56f7447}{if} you obey \char`\"{}make check\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}make test\char`\"{}. For other \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_abadea333aa49e0a4790a0567236a2e81}{environments}, see the \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a8a5001d171323f53bb8190b20d31beea}{instructions} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} N\+ON-\/A\+U\+T\+O\+T\+O\+O\+LS-\/B\+U\+I\+L\+D. The Run\+Test \hyperlink{basic-configuration_8txt_ac1048f198f179d52eda77c5ed6ab9ba9}{script} runs the \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a484396302564f57b7646cfd198092762}{pcretest} test \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a48917cf15a1089461e55bc56de9a58c3}{program} (\hyperlink{README_8txt_a9d3df0d4bed2ac7e1c01860363ab4ac2}{which} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} documented \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} its own \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a0ccf45b17b45fe5e9f9dbe203ebd801a}{man} page) \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_gade8f959a935ed315f9f55422c7de9903}{on} each \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the relevant testinput \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a5aaeef01bce395cfcb41dd64a3bf8607}{files} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} the testdata \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ac33d049ccd70185ffba7bed3d06d9ea2}{directory}, and compares the \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_acf47d950a4853a501d6b975b394de5e5}{output} \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} the contents \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the corresponding testoutput files. Run\+Test uses \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ac062b5382a17ef4e936c49bdd74c5563}{file} called testtry \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} hold the \hyperlink{time-sem_8c_a70db8bd1d499619f7ff9c1ca2ff3c8df}{main} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_acf47d950a4853a501d6b975b394de5e5}{output} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a900bb06a4314d99c8ad08d1ceffd114e}{from} pcretest. Other \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a5aaeef01bce395cfcb41dd64a3bf8607}{files} whose \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a0329fb20db61aae75d49812105cad192}{names} begin \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} \char`\"{}test\char`\"{} are \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ac199431a7baad211fadcdb6c45bfe7c0}{used} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7681723cb91eaa99771ee87f8465c1aa}{as} working \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a5aaeef01bce395cfcb41dd64a3bf8607}{files} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} some tests. Some \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} relevant only when certain build-\/\hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aafdc0b2481cb13eb2e0183db31aa1c5d}{time} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aefb1fa742c21909e746b978f6e1d7e17}{options} were selected. For \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ac2cc8dc0b2cf1d8e2d04667390da7402}{example}, the \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} for U\+TF-\/8/16/32 \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ad138d584026b091836ba441440a66ff5}{support} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} only \hyperlink{util__expr__scan_8c_aa1a71763978093648dffef60b56f7447}{if} -\/-\/enable-\/utf was used. Run\+Test outputs \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} comment when \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it} skips \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} test. Many \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} that \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aab236af6334f68eebb41dff13921475a}{not} skipped \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} up \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} three times. The \hyperlink{group__apr__tables_gade8df35e4d83c24788cf409262f7fc51}{second} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} forces \hyperlink{pcre__study_8c_a5ddb6003cb295c71d266484df6bcda0b}{pcre\+\_\+study}() \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ac08ce70cbd4f453457597ad15ecbebdd}{be} called for \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a0c81554ea08028a00dbedabe60072c53}{all} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_aca23d6bf5b793a5e2a75a714f962e664}{patterns} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad8436ab6efaeffcb6849cd61d730eb30}{except} for \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} few \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} some \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} that \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} marked \char`\"{}never \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ad3e0d03c4531f529451b54c48ee48bb6}{study}\char`\"{} (see the \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a484396302564f57b7646cfd198092762}{pcretest} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a48917cf15a1089461e55bc56de9a58c3}{program} for \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga6e0837f31f9838d1bc93f4e98184579f}{how} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a1d4586f0a85ecec85237e5fb0f611dd1}{this} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{ab_8c_a5992b274cfdcacdbc1fa8347fd01ebde}{done}). If J\+IT \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ad138d584026b091836ba441440a66ff5}{support} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a4535630baf343422449d0c4d3f6d0ae7}{available}, the non-\/D\+FA \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} third \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aafdc0b2481cb13eb2e0183db31aa1c5d}{time}, \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a1d4586f0a85ecec85237e5fb0f611dd1}{this} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aafdc0b2481cb13eb2e0183db31aa1c5d}{time} \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} forced \hyperlink{pcre__study_8c_a5ddb6003cb295c71d266484df6bcda0b}{pcre\+\_\+study}() \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} the \hyperlink{pcre_8h_adb2a713b53698607ab6816aa6a7c6c21}{P\+C\+R\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+U\+D\+Y\+\_\+\+J\+I\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+I\+LE} option. This testing \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a2a892895a50bc58f3679c7acb58190e6}{can} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ac08ce70cbd4f453457597ad15ecbebdd}{be} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a6ab3b4135a5a5c7be5906d3ee5df7724}{suppressed} by putting \char`\"{}nojit\char`\"{} on the Run\+Test \hyperlink{README_8txt_ad096865ab7f15682efeeeb3ef7983ae3}{command} line. The entire \hyperlink{README_8txt_af5b772536a61c888f9b40122c9816047}{set} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_aab182d126ab6b06fdffef58b1a664ca1}{once} for each \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the 8-\/\hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aeddb586b79a44fb202dde924852cbbf6}{bit}, 16-\/\hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aeddb586b79a44fb202dde924852cbbf6}{bit} and 32-\/\hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aeddb586b79a44fb202dde924852cbbf6}{bit} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ae4aecc72ae4789d0b7d4d9280e7679a1}{libraries} that \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} enabled. If you want \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} just one \hyperlink{README_8txt_af5b772536a61c888f9b40122c9816047}{set} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests}, call Run\+Test \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} either the -\/8, -\/16 \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a1e1dbf0220a28f9a8c394172dd6da171}{or} -\/32 option. If valgrind \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{README_8txt_abf5a4a7b9414b8b9683ee861c8a64879}{installed}, you \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a2a892895a50bc58f3679c7acb58190e6}{can} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} the \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} under \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it} by putting \char`\"{}valgrind\char`\"{} on the Run\+Test \hyperlink{README_8txt_ad096865ab7f15682efeeeb3ef7983ae3}{command} line. To \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a484396302564f57b7646cfd198092762}{pcretest} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_gade8f959a935ed315f9f55422c7de9903}{on} just one \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a1e1dbf0220a28f9a8c394172dd6da171}{or} more specific test \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a5aaeef01bce395cfcb41dd64a3bf8607}{files}, give their numbers \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7681723cb91eaa99771ee87f8465c1aa}{as} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a10a3a3b838670cc298974841b7588803}{arguments} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} Run\+Test, for example\+: Run\+Test 2 7 11 You \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a2a892895a50bc58f3679c7acb58190e6}{can} also specify ranges \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} such \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7681723cb91eaa99771ee87f8465c1aa}{as} 3-\/6 \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a1e1dbf0220a28f9a8c394172dd6da171}{or} 3-\/ (meaning 3 \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} the \hyperlink{group__apr__strings_ga87c7e3f3f70b6e7de10e3f56e3f4d7a4}{end}), \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a1e1dbf0220a28f9a8c394172dd6da171}{or} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7965c027cf47c0c0e2396d2f8e6b40c3}{number} preceded by $\sim$ \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a7051e7217b0e2b72dfce35ad695b2b79}{exclude} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} test. For example\+: Runtest 3-\/15 $\sim$10 This runs \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} 3 \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} 15, excluding test 10, and just $\sim$13 runs \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a0c81554ea08028a00dbedabe60072c53}{all} the \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad8436ab6efaeffcb6849cd61d730eb30}{except} test 13. Whatever \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ac821da7698fda6b0bbdb81c9a4c6e339}{order} the \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a10a3a3b838670cc298974841b7588803}{arguments} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in}, the \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} always \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} numerical order. You \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a2a892895a50bc58f3679c7acb58190e6}{can} also call Run\+Test \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} the single \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a6f723bfa0cd83dd00f6e3df38741af6b}{argument} \char`\"{}list\char`\"{} to cause \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_acf47d950a4853a501d6b975b394de5e5}{output} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_aeb6b944e4524f915483b5696b7f2f424}{list} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} tests. The \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ae5e6e8bc4bfa800414992418716f96df}{first} test \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ac062b5382a17ef4e936c49bdd74c5563}{file} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a2a892895a50bc58f3679c7acb58190e6}{can} \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ac08ce70cbd4f453457597ad15ecbebdd}{be} fed directly into the \hyperlink{perltest_8txt_a841c59daab01e1f609fdd4547afbe6e6}{perltest.\+pl} \hyperlink{basic-configuration_8txt_ac1048f198f179d52eda77c5ed6ab9ba9}{script} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} check that \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ab4ce39be83e35c074153e23755e6b420}{Perl} gives the same results. The only difference you should see \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} the \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_ae5e6e8bc4bfa800414992418716f96df}{first} few \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a0fcc426e1c273f0ffcfbd2e3b2412ac3}{lines}, \hyperlink{group__apr__network__io_ga40101ce9c63cc7ab2b80f6f8c0e7086c}{where} the \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ab4ce39be83e35c074153e23755e6b420}{Perl} version \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a9dffb3dde41716fc3bef8d0ee982f378}{given} instead \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} version. The \hyperlink{group__apr__tables_gade8df35e4d83c24788cf409262f7fc51}{second} \hyperlink{README_8txt_af5b772536a61c888f9b40122c9816047}{set} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{running-developer-tests_8txt_ae0edb32d329db43bf8a0513c0967e5b9}{tests} check \hyperlink{pcre__fullinfo_8c_afb0823d0be4280eb7a36661841375b71}{pcre\+\_\+fullinfo}(), \hyperlink{pcre__study_8c_a5ddb6003cb295c71d266484df6bcda0b}{pcre\+\_\+study}(), \hyperlink{pcre__get_8c_a169e8ba42601e29fbd4ef694b0ced2fe}{pcre\+\_\+copy\+\_\+substring}(), \hyperlink{pcre__get_8c_ad3b53656dd1dcf177e8b6df0452ef06f}{pcre\+\_\+get\+\_\+substring}(), \hyperlink{pcre__get_8c_a789e9042a0d4e1ec35ae32732a786b39}{pcre\+\_\+get\+\_\+substring\+\_\+list}(), \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a49f154ded02555c4d15e7861acf2e434}{error} detection, and \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a5a989107465910839d799cefcea80d85}{run}-\/\hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aafdc0b2481cb13eb2e0183db31aa1c5d}{time} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7a10cd81a384ff727296d05bb827806}{flags} that \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a98da773651c0ef9992aa9a7bab588058}{are} specific \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE}, \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7681723cb91eaa99771ee87f8465c1aa}{as} well \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a7681723cb91eaa99771ee87f8465c1aa}{as} the P\+O\+S\+IX wrapper A\+P\+I. It also uses the debugging \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7a10cd81a384ff727296d05bb827806}{flags} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_aa22c98f630e4b3fe86ee17ce5150c62f}{to} check some \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} the internals \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{pcre__compile_8c_a73bc1d517e53ae9e6e8c51075f9ac72a}{pcre\+\_\+compile}(). If you build \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a970782a5ef22596881e664deb789f171}{P\+C\+RE} \hyperlink{group__apr__atomic_ga62bdcea60b77e638d3d88947a34aff05}{with} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a841271aab70f5cda9412a19c7753f02c}{a} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_abd47f5cbdb1ec8253aaff6092114af6a}{locale} \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a935b0b98e07f1e5b6c06e9821ff32fec}{setting} that \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a2569119f3fd3f0d7d7ecea3c96acb0bf}{is} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_aab236af6334f68eebb41dff13921475a}{not} the standard \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ac5c2ebe543528426f0c731e1b7056868}{C} \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_abd47f5cbdb1ec8253aaff6092114af6a}{locale}, the \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_a519ab140d596a5da5fffad3abf3d5d6d}{character} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a0a3ce7ba2875673af4ff52c60636a7cb}{tables} may \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ac08ce70cbd4f453457597ad15ecbebdd}{be} different (see next paragraph). In some \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a23959172d6d08608d9a83d27016a1b4e}{cases}, \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a1d4586f0a85ecec85237e5fb0f611dd1}{this} may cause failures \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} the \hyperlink{group__apr__tables_gade8df35e4d83c24788cf409262f7fc51}{second} \hyperlink{README_8txt_af5b772536a61c888f9b40122c9816047}{set} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} tests. \subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Dregcomp}{Dregcomp}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}using {\bf Dregcomp} =  P\+C\+R\+Eregcomp (and similarly for the other P\+O\+S\+IX {\bf functions}) {\bf to} the {\bf compiler} {\bf flags} ({\bf C\+F\+L\+A\+GS} {\bf if} you {\bf are} using \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} -\/-\/ see {\bf below}). This has the effect {\bf of} renaming the {\bf functions} {\bf so} that the {\bf names} no longer clash. Of {\bf course}, you have {\bf to} {\bf do} the same thing for your {\bf applications}, {\bf or} write {\bf them} using the new names. Documentation for {\bf P\+C\+RE} -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ If you {\bf install} {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf in} the normal {\bf way} {\bf on} {\bf a} Unix-\/like {\bf system}, you will {\bf end} up {\bf with} {\bf a} {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf man} {\bf pages} whose {\bf names} {\bf all} {\bf start} {\bf with} \char`\"{}pcre\char`\"{}. The one that {\bf is} just called \char`\"{}pcre\char`\"{} lists {\bf all} the others. In {\bf addition} {\bf to} these {\bf man} {\bf pages}, the {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf documentation} {\bf is} supplied {\bf in} two other forms\+: 1. There {\bf are} {\bf files} called {\bf doc}/{\bf pcre.\+txt}, {\bf doc}/{\bf pcregrep.\+txt}, and {\bf doc}/{\bf pcretest.\+txt} {\bf in} the {\bf source} distribution. The {\bf first} {\bf of} these {\bf is} {\bf a} concatenation {\bf of} the {\bf text} forms {\bf of} {\bf all} the {\bf section} 3 {\bf man} {\bf pages} {\bf except} the listing {\bf of} {\bf pcredemo.\+c} and those that summarize individual functions. The other two {\bf are} the {\bf text} forms {\bf of} the {\bf section} 1 {\bf man} {\bf pages} for the pcregrep and {\bf pcretest} commands. These {\bf text} forms {\bf are} provided for ease {\bf of} {\bf scanning} {\bf with} {\bf text} editors {\bf or} similar tools. They {\bf are} {\bf installed} {\bf in} $<${\bf prefix}$>$/share/{\bf doc}/{\bf pcre}, {\bf where} $<${\bf prefix}$>$ {\bf is} the installation {\bf prefix} (defaulting {\bf to} /usr/local). 2. {\bf A} {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf files} containing {\bf all} the {\bf documentation} {\bf in} H\+T\+ML form, hyperlinked {\bf in} various ways, and rooted {\bf in} {\bf a} {\bf file} called index.\+html, {\bf is} {\bf distributed} {\bf in} {\bf doc}/html and {\bf installed} {\bf in} $<${\bf prefix}$>$/share/{\bf doc}/{\bf pcre}/html. Users {\bf of} {\bf P\+C\+RE} have contributed {\bf files} containing the {\bf documentation} for various releases {\bf in} C\+HM format. These {\bf can} {\bf be} {\bf found} {\bf in} the Contrib {\bf directory} {\bf of} the F\+TP {\bf site} (see next {\bf section}). Contributions by users {\bf of} {\bf P\+C\+RE} -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ You {\bf can} find contributions {\bf from} {\bf P\+C\+RE} users {\bf in} the {\bf directory} ftp\+: There {\bf is} {\bf a} R\+E\+A\+D\+ME {\bf file} giving brief descriptions {\bf of} {\bf what} they are. Some {\bf are} complete {\bf in} {\bf themselves}}\hypertarget{README_8txt_ae7677822fff7f2fa74781785b5dd78e7}{}\label{README_8txt_ae7677822fff7f2fa74781785b5dd78e7}
\index{R\+E\+A\+D\+M\+E.\+txt@{R\+E\+A\+D\+M\+E.\+txt}!L\+I\+BS@{L\+I\+BS}}
\index{L\+I\+BS@{L\+I\+BS}!R\+E\+A\+D\+M\+E.\+txt@{R\+E\+A\+D\+M\+E.\+txt}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{L\+I\+BS}{LIBS}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}using {\bf L\+I\+BS} =  \char`\"{}-\/lncurses\char`\"{} as well. This {\bf is} because, {\bf to} {\bf quote} the readline I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+LL, \char`\"{}Readline uses the termcap {\bf functions}, but does {\bf not} link {\bf with} the termcap {\bf or} curses {\bf library} {\bf itself}, allowing {\bf applications} {\bf which} link {\bf with} readline the {\bf to} choose an appropriate library.\char`\"{} If you get {\bf error} messages about missing {\bf functions} tgetstr, tgetent, tputs, tgetflag, {\bf or} tgoto, {\bf this} {\bf is} the problem, and linking {\bf with} the ncurses {\bf library} should fix it. The \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} script builds the following {\bf files} for the basic {\bf C} library\+: . Makefile the makefile that builds the {\bf library} . {\bf config.\+h} build-\/{\bf time} configuration {\bf options} for the {\bf library} . {\bf pcre.\+h} the public {\bf P\+C\+RE} header {\bf file} . {\bf pcre}-\/config {\bf script} that shows the building settings such {\bf as} {\bf C\+F\+L\+A\+GS} that were {\bf set} for \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} . libpcre.\+pc ) {\bf data} for the pkg-\/config {\bf command} . libpcre16.\+pc ) . libpcre32.\+pc ) . libpcreposix.\+pc ) . libtool {\bf script} that builds {\bf shared} and/{\bf or} static {\bf libraries} Versions {\bf of} {\bf config.\+h} and {\bf pcre.\+h} {\bf are} {\bf distributed} {\bf in} the {\bf P\+C\+RE} tarballs under the {\bf names} config.\+h.\+generic and pcre.\+h.\+generic. These {\bf are} provided for those who have {\bf to} {\bf built} {\bf P\+C\+RE} without using \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} or C\+Make. If you use \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} or C\+Make, the .generic versions {\bf are} {\bf not} used. When building the 8-\/{\bf bit} {\bf library}, {\bf if} {\bf a} {\bf C}++ {\bf compiler} {\bf is} {\bf found}, the following {\bf files} {\bf are} also built\+: . libpcrecpp.\+pc {\bf data} for the pkg-\/config {\bf command} . {\bf pcrecpparg.\+h} header {\bf file} for calling {\bf P\+C\+RE} via the {\bf C}++ wrapper . {\bf pcre\+\_\+stringpiece.\+h} header for the {\bf C}++ \char`\"{}stringpiece\char`\"{} functions The \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} script also creates {\bf config.\+status}, {\bf which} {\bf is} an executable {\bf script} that {\bf can} {\bf be} {\bf run} {\bf to} recreate the configuration, and config.\+log, {\bf which} {\bf contains} {\bf compiler} {\bf output} {\bf from} {\bf tests} that \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} runs. Once \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} has {\bf run}, you {\bf can} {\bf run} \char`\"{}make\char`\"{}. This builds the the {\bf libraries} {\bf libpcre}, {\bf libpcre16} and/{\bf or} {\bf libpcre32}, and {\bf a} test {\bf program} called pcretest. If you {\bf enabled} J\+IT {\bf support} {\bf with} -\/-\/enable-\/jit, {\bf a} test {\bf program} called pcre\+\_\+jit\+\_\+test {\bf is} {\bf built} {\bf as} well. If the 8-\/{\bf bit} {\bf library} {\bf is} {\bf built}, libpcreposix and the pcregrep {\bf command} {\bf are} also {\bf built}, and {\bf if} {\bf a} {\bf C}++ {\bf compiler} was {\bf found} {\bf on} your {\bf system}, and you did {\bf not} disable {\bf it} {\bf with} -\/-\/disable-\/cpp, \char`\"{}make\char`\"{} builds the {\bf C}++ wrapper {\bf library}, {\bf which} {\bf is} called libpcrecpp, {\bf as} well {\bf as} some test programs called pcrecpp\+\_\+unittest, pcre\+\_\+scanner\+\_\+unittest, and pcre\+\_\+stringpiece\+\_\+unittest. The {\bf command} \char`\"{}make check\char`\"{} runs {\bf all} the appropriate tests. Details {\bf of} the {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf tests} {\bf are} {\bf given} {\bf below} {\bf in} {\bf a} separate {\bf section} {\bf of} {\bf this} document. You {\bf can} use \char`\"{}make {\bf install}\char`\"{} to {\bf install} {\bf P\+C\+RE} into live {\bf directories} {\bf on} your system. The following {\bf are} {\bf installed} ({\bf file} {\bf names} {\bf are} {\bf all} relative {\bf to} the $<${\bf prefix}$>$ that {\bf is} {\bf set} when \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} is {\bf run})\+: Commands (bin)\+: {\bf pcretest} pcregrep ({\bf if} 8-\/{\bf bit} {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) {\bf pcre}-\/config Libraries ({\bf lib})\+: {\bf libpcre16} ({\bf if} 16-\/{\bf bit} {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) {\bf libpcre32} ({\bf if} 32-\/{\bf bit} {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) {\bf libpcre} ({\bf if} 8-\/{\bf bit} {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) libpcreposix ({\bf if} 8-\/{\bf bit} {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) libpcrecpp ({\bf if} 8-\/{\bf bit} and {\bf C}++ {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) Configuration information ({\bf lib}/pkgconfig)\+: libpcre16.\+pc libpcre32.\+pc libpcre.\+pc libpcreposix.\+pc libpcrecpp.\+pc ({\bf if} {\bf C}++ {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}) Header {\bf files} ({\bf include})\+: {\bf pcre.\+h} {\bf pcreposix.\+h} {\bf pcre\+\_\+scanner.\+h} ) {\bf pcre\+\_\+stringpiece.\+h} ) {\bf if} {\bf C}++ {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled} {\bf pcrecpp.\+h} ) {\bf pcrecpparg.\+h} ) Man {\bf pages} (share/{\bf man}/{\bf man}\{1,3\})\+: pcregrep.\+1 pcretest.\+1 {\bf pcre}-\/config.\+1 pcre.\+3 {\bf pcre}$\ast$.\+3 (lots more {\bf pages}, {\bf all} starting \char`\"{}pcre\char`\"{}) H\+T\+ML {\bf documentation} (share/{\bf doc}/{\bf pcre}/html)\+: index.\+html $\ast$.html (lots more {\bf pages}, hyperlinked {\bf from} index.\+html) Text {\bf file} {\bf documentation} (share/{\bf doc}/{\bf pcre})\+: A\+U\+T\+H\+O\+RS C\+O\+P\+Y\+I\+NG Change\+Log L\+I\+C\+E\+N\+CE N\+E\+WS R\+E\+A\+D\+ME {\bf pcre.\+txt} ({\bf a} concatenation {\bf of} the {\bf man}(3) {\bf pages}) {\bf pcretest.\+txt} the {\bf pcretest} {\bf man} page {\bf pcregrep.\+txt} the pcregrep {\bf man} page {\bf pcre}-\/{\bf config.\+txt} the {\bf pcre}-\/config {\bf man} page If you want {\bf to} {\bf remove} {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf from} your {\bf system}, you {\bf can} {\bf run} \char`\"{}make uninstall\char`\"{}. This removes {\bf all} the {\bf files} that \char`\"{}make {\bf install}\char`\"{} installed. {\bf However}, {\bf it} does {\bf not} {\bf remove} {\bf any} {\bf directories}, because these {\bf are} often {\bf shared} {\bf with} other programs. Retrieving configuration information -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ Running \char`\"{}make {\bf install}\char`\"{} installs the {\bf command} {\bf pcre}-\/config, {\bf which} {\bf can} {\bf be} {\bf used} {\bf to} recall information about the {\bf P\+C\+RE} configuration and installation. For example\+: {\bf pcre}-\/config -\/-\/version prints the version {\bf number}, and {\bf pcre}-\/config -\/-\/libs outputs information about {\bf where} the {\bf library} {\bf is} installed. This {\bf command} {\bf can} {\bf be} {\bf included} {\bf in} makefiles for programs that use {\bf P\+C\+RE}, saving the programmer {\bf from} having {\bf to} remember too many details. The pkg-\/config {\bf command} {\bf is} {\bf another} {\bf system} for saving and retrieving information about {\bf installed} libraries. {\bf Instead} {\bf of} separate commands for each {\bf library}, {\bf a} single {\bf command} {\bf is} used. For example\+: pkg-\/config -\/-\/{\bf cflags} {\bf pcre} The {\bf data} {\bf is} held {\bf in} $\ast$.pc {\bf files} that {\bf are} {\bf installed} {\bf in} {\bf a} {\bf directory} called $<${\bf prefix}$>$/{\bf lib}/pkgconfig. Shared {\bf libraries} -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ The {\bf default} distribution builds {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf as} {\bf shared} {\bf libraries} and static {\bf libraries}, {\bf as} long {\bf as} the operating {\bf system} supports {\bf shared} libraries. Shared {\bf library} {\bf support} relies {\bf on} the \char`\"{}libtool\char`\"{} script {\bf which} {\bf is} {\bf built} {\bf as} part {\bf of} the \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} process. The libtool {\bf script} {\bf is} {\bf used} {\bf to} {\bf compile} and link both {\bf shared} and static libraries. They {\bf are} placed {\bf in} {\bf a} subdirectory called .libs when they {\bf are} newly built. The programs {\bf pcretest} and pcregrep {\bf are} {\bf built} {\bf to} use these uninstalled {\bf libraries} (by means {\bf of} wrapper {\bf scripts} {\bf in} the {\bf case} {\bf of} {\bf shared} {\bf libraries}). When you use \char`\"{}make {\bf install}\char`\"{} to {\bf install} {\bf shared} {\bf libraries}, pcregrep and {\bf pcretest} {\bf are} automatically {\bf re}-\/{\bf built} {\bf to} use the newly {\bf installed} {\bf shared} {\bf libraries} before being {\bf installed} themselves. {\bf However}, the versions left {\bf in} the build {\bf directory} {\bf still} use the uninstalled libraries. To build {\bf P\+C\+RE} using static {\bf libraries} only you must use -\/-\/disable-\/{\bf shared} when configuring it. For example\+: ./{\bf configure} -\/-\/{\bf prefix}=/usr/gnu -\/-\/disable-\/{\bf shared} Then {\bf run} \char`\"{}make\char`\"{} in the usual way. {\bf Similarly}, you {\bf can} use -\/-\/disable-\/static {\bf to} build only {\bf shared} libraries. Cross-\/{\bf compiling} using autotools -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ You {\bf can} specify CC and {\bf C\+F\+L\+A\+GS} {\bf in} the normal {\bf way} {\bf to} the \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} command, {\bf in} {\bf order} {\bf to} cross-\/{\bf compile} {\bf P\+C\+RE} for some other host. {\bf However}, you should N\+OT specify -\/-\/enable-\/rebuild-\/{\bf chartables}, because {\bf if} you {\bf do}, the {\bf dftables.\+c} {\bf source} {\bf file} {\bf is} {\bf compiled} and {\bf run} {\bf on} the local {\bf host}, {\bf in} {\bf order} {\bf to} generate the inbuilt {\bf character} {\bf tables} (the {\bf pcre\+\_\+chartables.\+c} {\bf file}). This will probably {\bf not} work, because {\bf dftables.\+c} needs {\bf to} {\bf be} {\bf compiled} {\bf with} the local {\bf compiler}, {\bf not} the cross compiler. When -\/-\/enable-\/rebuild-\/{\bf chartables} {\bf is} {\bf not} {\bf specified}, {\bf pcre\+\_\+chartables.\+c} {\bf is} created by making {\bf a} copy {\bf of} {\bf pcre\+\_\+chartables.\+c.\+dist}, {\bf which} {\bf is} {\bf a} {\bf default} {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf tables} that assumes {\bf A\+S\+C\+II} code. Cross-\/{\bf compiling} {\bf with} the {\bf default} {\bf tables} should {\bf not} {\bf be} {\bf a} problem. If you need {\bf to} modify the {\bf character} {\bf tables} when cross-\/{\bf compiling}, you should move {\bf pcre\+\_\+chartables.\+c.\+dist} {\bf out} {\bf of} the {\bf way}, then {\bf compile} {\bf dftables.\+c} by hand and {\bf run} {\bf it} {\bf on} the local {\bf host} {\bf to} {\bf make} {\bf a} new version {\bf of} pcre\+\_\+chartables.\+c.\+dist. Then when you cross-\/{\bf compile} {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf this} new version {\bf of} the {\bf tables} will {\bf be} used. Using HP\textquotesingle{}{\bf s} A\+N\+SI {\bf C}++ {\bf compiler} (a\+CC) -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ Unless {\bf C}++ {\bf support} {\bf is} disabled by {\bf specifying} the \char`\"{}-\/-\/disable-\/cpp\char`\"{} option {\bf of} the \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} script, you must {\bf include} the \char`\"{}-\/AA\char`\"{} option {\bf in} the C\+X\+X\+F\+L\+A\+GS {\bf environment} variable {\bf in} {\bf order} for the {\bf C}++ components {\bf to} {\bf compile} correctly. Also, note that the a\+CC {\bf compiler} {\bf on} PA-\/R\+I\+SC platforms may have {\bf a} defect whereby needed {\bf libraries} {\bf fail} {\bf to} get {\bf included} when {\bf specifying} the \char`\"{}-\/AA\char`\"{} compiler option. If you experience unresolved symbols when linking the {\bf C}++ programs, use the workaround {\bf of} {\bf specifying} the following {\bf environment} variable prior {\bf to} running the \char`\"{}configure\char`\"{} script\+: C\+X\+X\+L\+D\+F\+L\+A\+GS=\char`\"{}-\/lstd\+\_\+v2 -\/l\+Csup\+\_\+v2\char`\"{} Compiling {\bf in} Tru64 using native compilers -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ The following {\bf error} may {\bf occur} when {\bf compiling} {\bf with} native compilers {\bf in} the Tru64 operating system\+: C\+XX libpcrecpp\+\_\+la-\/pcrecpp.\+lo cxx\+: Error\+: /usr/{\bf lib}/cmplrs/cxx/V7.\+1-\/006/{\bf include}/cxx/iosfwd, {\bf line} 58\+: \#{\bf error} directive\+: \char`\"{}cannot {\bf include} iosfwd -\/-\/ define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+D\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+T\+R\+E\+AM {\bf to} {\bf override} {\bf default} -\/ see {\bf section} 7.\+1.\+2 {\bf of} the {\bf C}++ Using Guide\char`\"{} -\/ see {\bf section} 7.\+1.\+2 {\bf of} the {\bf C}++ Using Guide\char`\"{} This may {\bf be} followed by other {\bf errors}, complaining that \textquotesingle{}namespace \char`\"{}std\char`\"{} has no member\textquotesingle{}. The solution {\bf to} {\bf this} {\bf is} {\bf to} add the {\bf line} \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+D\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+T\+R\+E\+AM 1 {\bf to} the {\bf config.\+h} file. Using Sun\textquotesingle{}{\bf s} compilers for Solaris -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ {\bf A} user reports that the following configurations work {\bf on} Solaris 9 sparcv9 and Solaris 9 {\bf x86} (32-\/{\bf bit})\+: Solaris 9 sparcv9\+: ./{\bf configure} -\/-\/disable-\/cpp CC=/bin/cc {\bf C\+F\+L\+A\+GS}=\char`\"{}-\/m64 -\/{\bf g}\char`\"{} Solaris 9 x86\+: ./{\bf configure} -\/-\/disable-\/cpp CC=/bin/cc {\bf C\+F\+L\+A\+GS}=\char`\"{}-\/g\char`\"{} Using {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf from} My\+S\+QL -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ On {\bf systems} {\bf where} both {\bf P\+C\+RE} and My\+S\+QL {\bf are} {\bf installed}, {\bf it} {\bf is} {\bf possible} {\bf to} {\bf make} use {\bf of} {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf from} within My\+S\+QL, {\bf as} an alternative {\bf to} the {\bf built}-\/{\bf in} {\bf pattern} matching. There {\bf is} {\bf a} web page that tells you {\bf how} {\bf to} {\bf do} this\+: http\+: Making new tarballs -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ The {\bf command} \char`\"{}make {\bf dist}\char`\"{} creates three {\bf P\+C\+RE} tarballs, {\bf in} tar.\+gz, {\bf tar.\+bz2}, and zip formats. The {\bf command} \char`\"{}make distcheck\char`\"{} does the same, but then does {\bf a} trial build {\bf of} the new distribution {\bf to} ensure that {\bf it} works. If you have modified {\bf any} {\bf of} the {\bf man} page sources {\bf in} the {\bf doc} {\bf directory}, you should {\bf first} {\bf run} the Prepare\+Release {\bf script} before making {\bf a} distribution. This {\bf script} creates the .{\bf txt} and H\+T\+ML forms {\bf of} the {\bf documentation} {\bf from} the {\bf man} pages. Testing {\bf P\+C\+RE} -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ To test the basic {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf library} {\bf on} {\bf a} Unix-\/like {\bf system}, {\bf run} the Run\+Test script. There {\bf is} {\bf another} {\bf script} called Run\+Grep\+Test that {\bf tests} the {\bf options} {\bf of} the pcregrep command. If the {\bf C}++ wrapper {\bf library} {\bf is} {\bf built}, three test programs called pcrecpp\+\_\+unittest, pcre\+\_\+scanner\+\_\+unittest, and pcre\+\_\+stringpiece\+\_\+unittest {\bf are} also built. When J\+IT {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf enabled}, {\bf another} test {\bf program} called pcre\+\_\+jit\+\_\+test {\bf is} built. Both the {\bf scripts} and {\bf all} the {\bf program} {\bf tests} {\bf are} {\bf run} {\bf if} you obey \char`\"{}make check\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}make test\char`\"{}. For other {\bf environments}, see the {\bf instructions} {\bf in} N\+ON-\/A\+U\+T\+O\+T\+O\+O\+LS-\/B\+U\+I\+L\+D. The Run\+Test {\bf script} runs the {\bf pcretest} test {\bf program} ({\bf which} {\bf is} documented {\bf in} its own {\bf man} page) {\bf on} each {\bf of} the relevant testinput {\bf files} {\bf in} the testdata {\bf directory}, and compares the {\bf output} {\bf with} the contents {\bf of} the corresponding testoutput files. Run\+Test uses {\bf a} {\bf file} called testtry {\bf to} hold the {\bf main} {\bf output} {\bf from} pcretest. Other {\bf files} whose {\bf names} begin {\bf with} \char`\"{}test\char`\"{} are {\bf used} {\bf as} working {\bf files} {\bf in} some tests. Some {\bf tests} {\bf are} relevant only when certain build-\/{\bf time} {\bf options} were selected. For {\bf example}, the {\bf tests} for U\+TF-\/8/16/32 {\bf support} {\bf are} {\bf run} only {\bf if} -\/-\/enable-\/utf was used. Run\+Test outputs {\bf a} comment when {\bf it} skips {\bf a} test. Many {\bf of} the {\bf tests} that {\bf are} {\bf not} skipped {\bf are} {\bf run} up {\bf to} three times. The {\bf second} {\bf run} forces {\bf pcre\+\_\+study}() {\bf to} {\bf be} called for {\bf all} {\bf patterns} {\bf except} for {\bf a} few {\bf in} some {\bf tests} that {\bf are} marked \char`\"{}never {\bf study}\char`\"{} (see the {\bf pcretest} {\bf program} for {\bf how} {\bf this} {\bf is} {\bf done}). If J\+IT {\bf support} {\bf is} {\bf available}, the non-\/D\+FA {\bf tests} {\bf are} {\bf run} {\bf a} third {\bf time}, {\bf this} {\bf time} {\bf with} {\bf a} forced {\bf pcre\+\_\+study}() {\bf with} the {\bf P\+C\+R\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+U\+D\+Y\+\_\+\+J\+I\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+P\+I\+LE} option. This testing {\bf can} {\bf be} {\bf suppressed} by putting \char`\"{}nojit\char`\"{} on the Run\+Test {\bf command} line. The entire {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf tests} {\bf is} {\bf run} {\bf once} for each {\bf of} the 8-\/{\bf bit}, 16-\/{\bf bit} and 32-\/{\bf bit} {\bf libraries} that {\bf are} enabled. If you want {\bf to} {\bf run} just one {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf tests}, call Run\+Test {\bf with} either the -\/8, -\/16 {\bf or} -\/32 option. If valgrind {\bf is} {\bf installed}, you {\bf can} {\bf run} the {\bf tests} under {\bf it} by putting \char`\"{}valgrind\char`\"{} on the Run\+Test {\bf command} line. To {\bf run} {\bf pcretest} {\bf on} just one {\bf or} more specific test {\bf files}, give their numbers {\bf as} {\bf arguments} {\bf to} Run\+Test, for example\+: Run\+Test 2 7 11 You {\bf can} also specify ranges {\bf of} {\bf tests} such {\bf as} 3-\/6 {\bf or} 3-\/ (meaning 3 {\bf to} the {\bf end}), {\bf or} {\bf a} {\bf number} preceded by $\sim$ {\bf to} {\bf exclude} {\bf a} test. For example\+: Runtest 3-\/15 $\sim$10 This runs {\bf tests} 3 {\bf to} 15, excluding test 10, and just $\sim$13 runs {\bf all} the {\bf tests} {\bf except} test 13. Whatever {\bf order} the {\bf arguments} {\bf are} {\bf in}, the {\bf tests} {\bf are} always {\bf run} {\bf in} numerical order. You {\bf can} also call Run\+Test {\bf with} the single {\bf argument} \char`\"{}list\char`\"{} to cause {\bf it} {\bf to} {\bf output} {\bf a} {\bf list} {\bf of} tests. The {\bf first} test {\bf file} {\bf can} {\bf be} fed directly into the {\bf perltest.\+pl} {\bf script} {\bf to} check that {\bf Perl} gives the same results. The only difference you should see {\bf is} {\bf in} the {\bf first} few {\bf lines}, {\bf where} the {\bf Perl} version {\bf is} {\bf given} instead {\bf of} the {\bf P\+C\+RE} version. The {\bf second} {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf tests} check {\bf pcre\+\_\+fullinfo}(), {\bf pcre\+\_\+study}(), {\bf pcre\+\_\+copy\+\_\+substring}(), {\bf pcre\+\_\+get\+\_\+substring}(), {\bf pcre\+\_\+get\+\_\+substring\+\_\+list}(), {\bf error} detection, and {\bf run}-\/{\bf time} {\bf flags} that {\bf are} specific {\bf to} {\bf P\+C\+RE}, {\bf as} well {\bf as} the P\+O\+S\+IX wrapper A\+P\+I. It also uses the debugging {\bf flags} {\bf to} check some {\bf of} the internals {\bf of} {\bf pcre\+\_\+compile}(). If you build {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf with} {\bf a} {\bf locale} {\bf setting} that {\bf is} {\bf not} the standard {\bf C} {\bf locale}, the {\bf character} {\bf tables} may {\bf be} different (see next paragraph). In some {\bf cases}, {\bf this} may cause failures {\bf in} the {\bf second} {\bf set} {\bf of} tests. For {\bf example}, {\bf in} {\bf a} {\bf locale} {\bf where} the isprint() {\bf function} yields {\bf T\+R\+UE} for {\bf characters} {\bf in} the range 128-\/255, the use {\bf of} \mbox{[}\+:isascii\+:\mbox{]} inside {\bf a} {\bf character} class defines {\bf a} different {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf characters}, and {\bf this} shows up {\bf in} {\bf this} test {\bf as} {\bf a} difference {\bf in} the {\bf compiled} {\bf code}, {\bf which} {\bf is} being listed for checking. Where the comparison test {\bf output} {\bf contains} \mbox{[}\textbackslash{}x00-\/\textbackslash{}x7f\mbox{]} the test will contain \mbox{[}\textbackslash{}x00-\/\textbackslash{}xff\mbox{]}, and similarly {\bf in} some other cases. This {\bf is} {\bf not} {\bf a} bug {\bf in} P\+C\+R\+E. The third {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf tests} checks {\bf pcre\+\_\+maketables}(), the {\bf facility} for building {\bf a} {\bf set} {\bf of} {\bf character} {\bf tables} for {\bf a} specific {\bf locale} and using {\bf them} instead {\bf of} the {\bf default} tables. The {\bf tests} {\bf make} use {\bf of} the \char`\"{}fr\+\_\+\+FR\char`\"{} (French) locale. Before running the test, the {\bf script} checks for the presence {\bf of} {\bf this} {\bf locale} by running the \char`\"{}locale\char`\"{} command. If that {\bf command} {\bf fails}, {\bf or} {\bf if} {\bf it} doesn\textquotesingle{}{\bf t} {\bf include} \char`\"{}fr\+\_\+\+FR\char`\"{} in the {\bf list} {\bf of} {\bf available} locales, the third test cannot {\bf be} {\bf run}, and {\bf a} comment {\bf is} {\bf output} {\bf to} say why. If running {\bf this} test produces instances {\bf of} the {\bf error} $\ast$$\ast$ Failed {\bf to} {\bf set} {\bf locale} \char`\"{}fr\+\_\+\+FR\char`\"{} in the comparison {\bf output}, {\bf it} means that {\bf locale} {\bf is} {\bf not} {\bf available} {\bf on} your {\bf system}, despite being listed by \char`\"{}locale\char`\"{}. This does {\bf not} mean that {\bf P\+C\+RE} {\bf is} broken. \mbox{[}If you {\bf are} trying {\bf to} {\bf run} {\bf this} test {\bf on} {\bf Windows}, you may {\bf be} {\bf able} {\bf to} get {\bf it} {\bf to} work by changing \char`\"{}fr\+\_\+\+FR\char`\"{} to \char`\"{}french\char`\"{} everywhere {\bf it} occurs. Alternatively, use Run\+Test.\+bat. The version {\bf of} {\bf Run\+Test.\+bat} {\bf included} {\bf with} {\bf P\+C\+RE} 7.\+4 and {\bf above} uses {\bf Windows} versions {\bf of} test 2. More {\bf info} {\bf on} using {\bf Run\+Test.\+bat} {\bf is} {\bf included} {\bf in} the {\bf document} entitled N\+ON-\/U\+N\+IX-\/U\+S\+E.\mbox{]} The fourth and fifth {\bf tests} check the U\+TF-\/8/16/32 {\bf support} and {\bf error} handling and internal U\+TF {\bf features} {\bf of} {\bf P\+C\+RE} that {\bf are} {\bf not} relevant {\bf to} {\bf Perl}, respectively. The sixth and seventh {\bf tests} {\bf do} the same for {\bf Unicode} {\bf character} properties support. The eighth, ninth, and tenth {\bf tests} check the {\bf pcre\+\_\+dfa\+\_\+exec}() alternative {\bf matching} {\bf function}, {\bf in} non-\/U\+TF-\/8/16/32 {\bf mode}, U\+TF-\/8/16/32 {\bf mode}, and U\+TF-\/8/16/32 {\bf mode} {\bf with} {\bf Unicode} property {\bf support}, respectively. The eleventh test checks some internal {\bf offsets} and {\bf code} {\bf size} {\bf features}}\hypertarget{README_8txt_a4fe02942dbea24d31d8c17a3ccb16449}{}\label{README_8txt_a4fe02942dbea24d31d8c17a3ccb16449}

{\bfseries Initial value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
=500

. \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a71e4557e7248fceb9478528030bfb7a5}{PCRE} has \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__FASTCGI_ga72a200675828d2c2550eb6c686b9db49}{a} counter that \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a13fc6af2ed5289933c1bccc61e950f56}{can} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a0f371a71e23776f0a08338302f581327}{be} \textcolor{keyword}{set} \hyperlink{group__MOD__PROXY_ga4d80b46c1e04eba6561893714933df30}{to} \hyperlink{README_8txt_aa4bc939c63755f8ebf214b60d65694b3}{limit} the amount \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} resources 
      \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it} uses
  when \hyperlink{pcregrep_8txt_a48f1285cbc2f880efa6527e2a20a2afa}{matching} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__FASTCGI_ga72a200675828d2c2550eb6c686b9db49}{a} \hyperlink{ap__regex_8h_a6e94763e2b1ed0b1fe86a58eb5e1eb73}{pattern}. If the \hyperlink{README_8txt_aa4bc939c63755f8ebf214b60d65694b3}{limit} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a7d947c770a43ed118ff283c41a1b303c}{is} exceeded during 
      \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__FASTCGI_ga72a200675828d2c2550eb6c686b9db49}{a} \hyperlink{README_8txt_ab4dbc9fcf813f9be3b8f4c7ef13868f7}{match}
\end{DoxyCode}

  \hyperlink{group__apr__network__io_gabc1e1b052bf705b27ebd2d24a96ec4d3}{on} the \textcolor{stringliteral}{"configure"} \hyperlink{README_8txt_ad096865ab7f15682efeeeb3ef7983ae3}{command}.

      \hyperlink{group__apr__thread__proc_ga2e46fea00cc2238744ebca5061c62bcc}{in} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__FASTCGI_ga72a200675828d2c2550eb6c686b9db49}{a}
  \hyperlink{ap__regex_8h_a6e94763e2b1ed0b1fe86a58eb5e1eb73}{pattern}. This limits the amount \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a9d5b55a535a7d176d14b62d664b47b4d}{of} \hyperlink{README_8txt_a2ef3475084e8c047fae1d0f5be26ff00}{system} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ab98e303524f0473011c8a87fcddb0e03}{stack} that \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__FASTCGI_ga72a200675828d2c2550eb6c686b9db49}{a} 
      \hyperlink{ap__regex_8h_a6e94763e2b1ed0b1fe86a58eb5e1eb73}{pattern} uses when \hyperlink{pcretest_8txt_ab977b64dbdb969ce031dc4281a792b3c}{it}
  \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a7d947c770a43ed118ff283c41a1b303c}{is} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_acf222623ce317d6483b477005378ffb0}{compiled}. The \textcolor{keywordflow}{default} \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_a7d947c770a43ed118ff283c41a1b303c}{is} 250
